Abstract: Multi-hop Question Answering (MHQA) aims to answer questions that require multi-step reasoning. It presents two key challenges: generating correct reasoning paths in response to the complex user queries, and accurately retrieving essential knowledge in the face of potential limitations in large language models (LLMs). Existing approaches primarily rely on prompt-based methods to generate reasoning paths, which are further combined with traditional sparse or dense retrieval to produce the final answer. However, the generation of reasoning paths commonly lacks effective control over the generative process, thus leading the reasoning astray. Meanwhile, the retrieval methods over-rely on knowledge matching or similarity scores rather than evaluating the practical utility of the information, resulting in retrieving homogeneous or non-useful information. Therefore, we propose a Structured Entity-Aware Retrieval with Chain-of-Reasoning Navigator framework named SEARCH-R. Moreover, a novel dependency tree-based retrieval is designed to evaluate the informational contribution of the document quantitatively. Abstract: Chart-to-code generation converts a chart image into an executable plotting script, enabling faithful reproduction and editable visualizations. ### [309] [MEG-RAG: Quantifying Multi-modal Evidence Grounding for Evidence Selection in RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24564)
*Xihang Wang,Zihan Wang,Chengkai Huang,Quan Z. Sheng,Lina Yao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了MEG与MEG-RAG方法，以提升多模态检索增强生成（MRAG）系统对检索证据的语义关联性和有效性判断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态检索增强生成系统很难判断检索到的多模态数据是否真正支持答案的语义核心，通常只依据启发式置信度等表浅指标，导致准确性不足。

Method: 作者提出了Multi-modal Evidence Grounding（MEG），这是一种语义感知型指标，能够量化检索证据对答案语义核心的贡献。MEG通过语义锚定（Semantic Certainty Anchoring），重点挖掘高-IDF的高信息量token，识别与答案语义核心密切相关的信息。在此基础上，作者设计了MEG-RAG框架，通过训练多模态重排序器，使得检索证据与标准答案的语义锚点更加一致。

Result: 在M$^2$RAG基准测试中，MEG-RAG在准确性和多模态一致性方面，均优于现有强基线，对不同教师模型具备良好泛化性。

Conclusion: MEG和MEG-RAG有助于提升多模态生成模型对检索证据语义价值的把控，有效提升生成答案的质量和一致性。

However, current MRAG systems struggle to distinguish whether retrieved multimodal data truly supports the semantic core of an answer or merely provides superficial relevance. Existing metrics often rely on heuristic position-based confidence, which fails to capture the informational density of multimodal entities. To address this, we propose Multi-modal Evidence Grounding (MEG), a semantic-aware metric that quantifies the contribution of retrieved evidence. Unlike standard confidence measures, MEG utilizes Semantic Certainty Anchoring, focusing on high-IDF information-bearing tokens that better capture the semantic core of the answer. Building on MEG, we introduce MEG-RAG, a framework that trains a multimodal reranker to align retrieved evidence with the semantic anchors of the ground truth. By prioritizing high-value content based on semantic grounding rather than token probability distributions, MEG-RAG improves the accuracy and multimodal consistency of generated outputs. Extensive experiments on the M$^2$RAG benchmark show that MEG-RAG consistently outperforms strong baselines and demonstrates robust generalization across different teacher models.

</details>


### [310] [Skill Retrieval Augmentation for Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24594)
*Weihang Su,Jianming Long,Qingyao Ai,Yichen Tang,Changyue Wang,Yiteng Tu,Yiqun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的大型语言模型（LLM）技能增强范式Skill Retrieval Augmentation（SRA），通过动态检索和应用外部技能库中的技能，有效扩展了模型能力，并引入SRA-Bench基准评估其效果。实验显示SRA能显著提升agent性能，但技能加载决策存在挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型向智能体方向发展，其需要借助大量外部技能处理本身能力范围外的任务。现有做法通过在上下文中枚举技能，不可扩展且易造成准确性下降。因此，亟需设计新的技能获取和利用机制。

Method: 作者提出Skill Retrieval Augmentation（SRA）范式，让agent在需要时从大规模外部技能库动态检索相应技能，并实现检索、整合和执行，同时设计了SRA-Bench基准用于解耦评估技能检索、整合和任务执行三个环节的表现。数据规模包含5400个测试任务、636个手工构造技能及超过2万混合干扰技能。

Result: 大量实验结果表明，基于检索的技能增强显著提升了agent在复杂任务中的表现。但也发现现有模型无论检索到真实技能与否，在是否需要外部能力时加载外部技能的频率相近，暴露出技能整合决策能力的不足。

Conclusion: SRA作为一种新颖有效的能力扩展方式能够大幅提升agent性能，但当前技术在有效决策是否需要外部技能加载上存在瓶颈，后续可在如何准确整合和选择外部技能方面深入研究，推动agent智能化和可扩展性发展。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) evolve into agentic problem solvers, they increasingly rely on external, reusable skills to handle tasks beyond their native parametric capabilities. In existing agent systems, the dominant strategy for incorporating skills is to explicitly enumerate available skills within the context window. However, this strategy fails to scale: as skill corpora expand, context budgets are consumed rapidly, and the agent becomes markedly less accurate in identifying the right skill. To this end, this paper formulates Skill Retrieval Augmentation (SRA), a new paradigm in which agents dynamically retrieve, incorporate, and apply relevant skills from large external skill corpora on demand. To make this problem measurable, we construct a large-scale skill corpus and introduce SRA-Bench, the first benchmark for decomposed evaluation of the full SRA pipeline, covering skill retrieval, skill incorporation, and end-task execution. SRA-Bench contains 5,400 capability-intensive test instances and 636 manually constructed gold skills, which are mixed with web-collected distractor skills to form a large-scale corpus of 26,262 skills. Extensive experiments show that retrieval-based skill augmentation can substantially improve agent performance, validating the promise of the paradigm. At the same time, we uncover a fundamental gap in skill incorporation: current LLM agents tend to load skills at similar rates, regardless of whether a gold skill is retrieved or whether the task actually requires external capabilities. This shows that the bottleneck in skill augmentation lies not only in retrieval but also in the base model's ability to determine which skill to load and when external loading is actually needed. These findings position SRA as a distinct research problem and establish a foundation for the scalable augmentation of capabilities in future agent systems.

Abstract: Many sign language translation (SLT) systems operate on pose sequences instead of raw video to reduce input dimensionality, improve portability, and partially anonymize signers. The choice of pose estimator is often treated as an implementation detail, with systems defaulting to widely available tools such as MediaPipe Holistic or OpenPose. We present a systematic comparison of pose estimators for pose-based SLT, covering widely used baselines (MediaPipe Holistic, OpenPose) and newer whole-body/high-capacity models (MMPose WholeBody, OpenPifPaf, AlphaPose, SDPose, Sapiens, SMPLest-X). We quantify downstream impact by training a controlled SLT pipeline on RWTH-PHOENIX-Weather 2014 where only the pose representation varies, evaluating with BLEU and BLEURT.
  To contextualize translation outcomes, we analyze temporal stability, missing hand keypoints, and robustness to occlusion using higher-resolution videos from the Signsuisse dataset. SDPose and Sapiens achieve the best translation performance (BLEU ~11.5), outperforming the common MediaPipe baseline (BLEU ~10). In occlusion cases, Sapiens is correct in all tested instances (15/15), while OpenPifPaf fails in nearly all (1/15) and also yields the weakest translation scores. Estimators that frequently leave out hand keypoints are associated with lower BLEU/BLEURT. We release code that can be used not only to reproduce our experiments, but also considerably lowers the barrier for other researchers to use alternative pose estimators.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Temporal relation classification is the task of determining the temporal relation between pairs of temporal entities in a text.
  Despite recent advancements in natural language processing, temporal relation classification remains a considerable challenge.
  Early attempts framed this task using a comprehensive set of temporal relations between events and temporal expressions.
  However, due to the task complexity, datasets have been progressively simplified, leading recent approaches to focus on the relations between event pairs and to use only a subset of relations.
  In this work, we revisit the broader goal of classifying interval relations between temporal entities by considering the full set of relations that can hold between two time intervals.
  The proposed approach, Interval from Point, involves first classifying the point relations between the endpoints of the temporal entities and then decoding these point relations into an interval relation.
  Evaluation on the TempEval-3 dataset shows that this approach can yield effective results, achieving a temporal awareness score of $70.1$ percent, a new state-of-the-art on this benchmark.

### [314] [DepthKV: Layer-Dependent KV Cache Pruning for Long-Context LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24647)
*Zahra Dehghanighobadi,Asja Fischer*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在长上下文推理中面临KV缓存内存消耗线性增长的问题，带来显著的推理内存瓶颈。现有缓存修剪方法未区分不同层对修剪的敏感性，普遍采用统一比例，可能影响模型性能。

Method: 提出DepthKV框架，依据各层对KV修剪的敏感性，分配整体KV缓存预算，实现层依赖的缓存修剪，而非统一修剪比例。

Result: 在多个模型和任务上，DepthKV相比统一修剪，在相同全局修剪比例下表现更优，KV预算利用更充分。

Conclusion: 不同层对KV修剪有不同敏感性，采用基于敏感性层依赖分配预算，可显著提升长上下文推理中KV修剪方法的效率与性能。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning is a critical capability of large language models (LLMs), enabling applications such as long-document understanding, summarization, and code generation. However, efficient autoregressive inference relies on the key-value (KV) cache, whose memory footprint grows linearly with sequence length, leading to a major memory bottleneck. To mitigate this overhead, KV cache pruning methods discard cached tokens with low attention scores during inference. Most existing methods apply a uniform pruning ratio across layers, implicitly assuming that all layers contribute equally to overall model performance. We show that this assumption is suboptimal, as layers differ significantly in their sensitivity to pruning. We propose DepthKV, a layer-dependent pruning framework that allocates a fixed global KV budget across layers based on their sensitivity, rather than using a uniform allocation. Across multiple models and tasks, DepthKV consistently outperforms uniform pruning at the same global pruning ratio, demonstrating more effective utilization of the KV cache budget through layer-dependent allocation.

### [315] [Benchmarking Source-Sensitive Reasoning in Turkish: Humans and LLMs under Evidential Trust Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24665)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来证据性语法标记与信息源真实性之间的关系受到关注，同时，AI 语言模型在理解复杂语用语法方面的表现也成为研究热点。土耳其语有独特的证据性后缀系统，对信息来源和信任度有区分，本研究旨在明确人类与LLMs在这一领域的能力差异。

Method: 首先进行人类实验，令土耳其语母语者在高信任与低信任语境下使用不同证据性后缀。随后测试10个主流LLMs在不同提示范式下（填空、显式时态填空、强迫选择）对类似语境的反应，并分析其输出的一致性及偏好。

Result: 人类实验显示，高信任语境显著提高-DI的使用，低信任则提高-mIs的比例，模式稳定。LLMs在不同模型与提示下表现各异，只出现微弱或局部一致性，整体不稳定，有时甚至反向，明显受到固有后缀偏好影响且常受任务合规性问题困扰。

Conclusion: 土耳其语母语者在证据性后缀选择上高度依赖对信息源的信任感，但目前的LLMs缺乏对这一语用-语法现象的深层次理解，表现出明显的人机差距。

Abstract: This paper investigates whether source trustworthiness shapes Turkish evidential morphology and whether large language models (LLMs) track this sensitivity. We study the past-domain contrast between -DI and -mIs in controlled cloze contexts where the information source is overtly external, while only its perceived reliability is manipulated (High-Trust vs. Low-Trust). In a human production experiment, native speakers of Turkish show a robust trust effect: High-Trust contexts yield relatively more -DI, whereas Low-Trust contexts yield relatively more -mIs, with the pattern remaining stable across sensitivity analyses. We then evaluate 10 LLMs in three prompting paradigms (open gap-fill, explicit past-tense gap-fill, and forced-choice A/B selection). LLM behavior is highly model- and prompt-dependent: some models show weak or local trust-consistent shifts, but effects are generally unstable, often reversed, and frequently overshadowed by output-compliance problems and strong base-rate suffix preferences. The results provide new evidence for a trust-/commitment-based account of Turkish evidentiality and reveal a clear human-LLM gap in source-sensitive evidential reasoning.

### [317] [Contextual Linear Activation Steering of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24693)

In this work, we introduce Contextual Linear Activation Steering (CLAS), a method that dynamically adapts linear activation steering to context-dependent steering strengths. Across eleven steering benchmarks and four model families, it consistently outperforms standard linear activation steering and matches or exceeds the performance of ReFT and LoRA in settings with limited labeled data. We therefore propose CLAS as a scalable, interpretable, and accurate method for specializing and steering large language models.

### [318] [The Chameleon's Limit: Investigating Persona Collapse and Homogenization in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24698)
*Yunze Xiao,Vivienne J. Zhang,Chenghao Yang,Ningshan Ma,Weihao Xuan,Jen-tse Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对基于大语言模型（LLMs）的多智能体应用中，个体性崩溃（Persona Collapse）现象进行了研究，提出了三个定量指标来评估群体多样性，并在多个任务和模型上验证了该现象的普遍性和复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体应用希望模拟现实社会中多样化的人群，但现实中常见的LLM往往导致模拟个体在行为与特征上趋于一致，缺乏应有的多样性。因此，研究这一问题对于提升基于LLM的群体模拟和社会系统研究具有重要意义。

Method: 作者提出了一个评估群体多样性的框架，包括三个维度：覆盖率（Coverage）、均匀性（Uniformity）和复杂性（Complexity），并用该框架对10种LLM在性格模拟、道德推理、自我介绍三项任务上进行了系统实验和分析。

Result: 实验发现，不同模型和任务下普遍存在“个体性崩溃”现象，表现为在部分维度或领域上多样性显著降低。同时，模型在任务上的高个体契合度不一定等于高多样性，群体行为往往陷入刻板印象而非真实个体差异。

Conclusion: 当前LLM难以在多智能体环境中产生真正多样、细腻的个体表现，高保真度反而带来刻板化风险，提示后续研究需关注群体层面多样性评估与提升。作者也发布了相关工具和数据以促进后续研究。

Abstract: Applications based on large language models (LLMs), such as multi-agent simulations, require population diversity among agents. We identify a pervasive failure mode we term \emph{Persona Collapse}: agents each assigned a distinct profile nonetheless converge into a narrow behavioral mode, producing a homogeneous simulated population. To quantify persona collapse, we propose a framework that measures how much of the persona space a population occupies (Coverage), how evenly agents spread across it (Uniformity), and how rich the resulting behavioral patterns are (Complexity). Evaluating ten LLMs on personality simulation (BFI-44), moral reasoning, and self-introduction, we observe persona collapse along two axes: (1) Dimensions: a model can appear diverse on one axis yet structurally degenerate on another, and (2) Domains: the same model may collapse the most in personality yet be the most diverse in moral reasoning. Furthermore, item-level diagnostics reveal that behavioral variation tracks coarse demographic stereotypes rather than the fine-grained individual differences specified in each persona. Counter-intuitively, \textbf{the models achieving the highest per-persona fidelity consistently produce the most stereotyped populations}. We release our toolkit and data to support population-level evaluation of LLMs.

</details>


### [319] [Green Shielding: A User-Centric Approach Towards Trustworthy AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24700)
*Aaron J. Li,Nicolas Sanchez,Hao Huang,Ruijiang Dong,Jaskaran Bains,Katrin Jaradeh,Zhen Xiang,Bo Li,Feng Liu,Aaron Kornblith,Bin Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）的输出对用户无意中的提问变化高度敏感，这直接影响了其在实际应用中的安全与效果。本文提出‘绿色护盾’（Green Shielding）理念，通过真实场景的微调方法和综合评估标准，系统测量和指导LLM在关键领域（如医疗）中的部署，以提高其稳定性和输出可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在实际部署中，输出常常因为用户表述的常规变化而有显著波动，尤其在医疗等高风险领域尤为突出。现有的红队测试主要针对恶意攻击，对于这种日常输入变化引发的风险关注不足，因此需有针对性地评估和指导。

Method: 提出‘绿色护盾’用户导向的部署评估框架，通过CUE准则（基于真实情景的基准、真实效用标准、真实提问方式下的扰动），联合临床医生开发了医疗诊断基准HCM-Dx，包含患者描述、结构化参考标准及临床相关的诊断质量评估方法，并系统分析了常规输入变化对诊断输出的影响。

Result: 多种前沿LLM在应对现实输入扰动时，诊断输出的主要维度发生系统性变化。中和操作（neutralization，即仅改变用户描述，不影响临床信息）会提升输出的合理性和专业性，但降低了对高风险和关键疾病的覆盖率。

Conclusion: 用户的输入方式会系统性地影响LLM诊断结果，因此需提供基于证据的用户指引以确保高风险领域部署的安全性。‘绿色护盾’框架不仅适用于医疗，还可推广到其他决策支持和智能体系统，提高LLM在实际场景下的可靠性和安全性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed, yet their outputs can be highly sensitive to routine, non-adversarial variation in how users phrase queries, a gap not well addressed by existing red-teaming efforts. We propose Green Shielding, a user-centric agenda for building evidence-backed deployment guidance by characterizing how benign input variation shifts model behavior. We operationalize this agenda through the CUE criteria: benchmarks with authentic Context, reference standards and metrics that capture true Utility, and perturbations that reflect realistic variations in the Elicitation of model behavior. Guided by the PCS framework and developed with practicing physicians, we instantiate Green Shielding in medical diagnosis through HealthCareMagic-Diagnosis (HCM-Dx), a benchmark of patient-authored queries, together with structured reference diagnosis sets and clinically grounded metrics for evaluating differential diagnosis lists. We also study perturbation regimes that capture routine input variation and show that prompt-level factors shift model behavior along clinically meaningful dimensions. Across multiple frontier LLMs, these shifts trace out Pareto-like tradeoffs. In particular, neutralization, which removes common user-level factors while preserving clinical content, increases plausibility and yields more concise, clinician-like differentials, but reduces coverage of highly likely and safety-critical conditions. Together, these results show that interaction choices can systematically shift task-relevant properties of model outputs and support user-facing guidance for safer deployment in high-stakes domains. Although instantiated here in medical diagnosis, the agenda extends naturally to other decision-support settings and agentic AI systems.

</details>


### [320] [Long-Context Aware Upcycling: A New Frontier for Hybrid LLM Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24715)
*Parsa Ashrafi Fashi,Utkarsh Saxena,Mehdi Rezagholizadeh,Aref Jafari,Akash Haridas,Mingyu Yang,Vansh Bhatia,Guihong Li,Vikram Appia,Emad Barsoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为HyLo的混合序列模型，可以在保留预训练Transformer模型优点的基础上，大幅提升模型的长上下文处理能力，并减少内存消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合序列模型大多需要从头预训练，无法复用已有的大型Transformer模型检查点，导致训练成本高且模型应用受限。因此，作者希望找到一种对现有Transformer模型“升级再造”的方法，提升其长上下文能力，同时继承其在短上下文下的表现。

Method: 提出HyLo混合架构，通过用高效的Transformer模块、多头潜在注意力（MLA）和线性模块（如Mamba2或Gated DeltaNet）对传统Transformer进行架构适配，再采用分阶段的长上下文训练和教师引导的蒸馏优化旧模型，实现了模型结构和训练流程的有效结合与优化。

Result: 通过后训练，HyLo将可用上下文长度扩展至原有的32倍，显著减少KV-cache内存消耗（降低90%以上），在vLLM推理系统中实现了高达2M tokens的prefill和decoding，而同规模Llama模型在64K context时已耗尽内存。HyLo在不同参数规模下（如基于Llama和Qwen的1B、3B模型）都展现了优异的短、长上下文能力，并在RULER等长上下文评测中大幅优于同类最先进的混合模型。尤其是HyLo-Qwen-1.7B只用10B数据训练，在多个评测上超越了用400B数据训练的JetNemotron。

Conclusion: HyLo为现有Transformer模型提供了一种低成本但高效的升级路径，在不牺牲短上下文性能的前提下显著提高了模型的长上下文能力和推理效率，展示了强大的扩展潜力和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Hybrid sequence models that combine efficient Transformer components with linear sequence modeling blocks are a promising alternative to pure Transformers, but most are still pretrained from scratch and therefore fail to reuse existing Transformer checkpoints. We study upcycling as a practical path to convert pretrained Transformer LLMs into hybrid architectures while preserving short-context quality and improving long-context capability. We call our solution \emph{HyLo} (HYbrid LOng-context): a long-context upcycling recipe that combines architectural adaptation with efficient Transformer blocks, Multi-Head Latent Attention (MLA), and linear blocks (Mamba2 or Gated DeltaNet), together with staged long-context training and teacher-guided distillation for stable optimization. HyLo extends usable context length by up to $32\times$ through efficient post-training and reduces KV-cache memory by more than $90\%$, enabling up to 2M-token prefill and decoding in our \texttt{vLLM} inference stack, while comparable Llama baselines run out of memory beyond 64K context. Across 1B- and 3B-scale settings (Llama- and Qwen-based variants), HyLo delivers consistently strong short- and long-context performance and significantly outperforms state-of-the-art upcycled hybrid baselines on long-context evaluations such as RULER. Notably, at similar scale, HyLo-Qwen-1.7B trained on only 10B tokens significantly outperforms JetNemotron (trained on 400B tokens) on GSM8K, Lm-Harness common sense reasoning and RULER-64K.

</details>


### [321] [Sentiment and Emotion Classification of Indonesian E-Commerce Reviews via Multi-Task BiLSTM and AutoML Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24720)
*Hermawan Manurung,Ibrahim Al-Kahfi,Ahmad Rizqi,Martin Clinton Tosima Manullang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对印尼电商评论中混合标准用语、俚语、方言借词、数字缩写和表情符号等复杂现象，开发了两条并行的情感和情绪分类流水线，大幅提升了自动分析的准确性和实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统词典驱动的情感分析工具在处理混杂语言（如印尼电商评论）时效果不佳，亟需更健壮、兼容多样语言特征的方法。

Method: 提出两条并行路径：第一条利用TF-IDF特征和PyCaret AutoML对多种标准分类器自动调参；第二条采用PyTorch实现的BiLSTM网络，具有共享编码器和两个专门用于二分类/五分类的输出头。清洗预处理包括14步和140条俚语词典，针对PRDECT-ID数据集训练，并与TextCNN等模型对比。

Result: 四种神经网络配置（BiLSTM Baseline、Improved、Large及TextCNN）均进行了基准测试，通过加权损失、学习率调度和早停机制优化，模型整体表现优异，在复杂评论环境下取得良好效果。所有流程以Gradio应用部署，代码开放。

Conclusion: 在印尼电商评论的多样性、噪声特征下，方法有效提升了情感与情绪识别的准确率，为类似多语用社交文本分析提供了可借鉴范式。

Abstract: Indonesian marketplace reviews mix standard vocabulary with slang, regional loanwords, numeric shorthands, and emoji, making lexicon-based sentiment tools unreliable in practice. This paper describes a two-track classification pipeline applied to the PRDECT-ID dataset, which contains 5,400 product reviews from 29 Indonesian e-commerce categories, each labeled for binary sentiment (Positive/Negative) and five-class emotion (Happy, Sad, Fear, Love, Anger). The first track applies TF-IDF vectorization with a PyCaret AutoML sweep across standard classifiers. The second track is a PyTorch Bidirectional Long Short-Term Memory (BiLSTM) network with a shared encoder and two task-specific output heads. A preprocessing module applies 14 sequential cleaning steps, including a 140-entry slang dictionary assembled from marketplace corpora. Four configurations are benchmarked: BiLSTM Baseline, BiLSTM Improved, BiLSTM Large, and TextCNN. Training uses class-weighted cross-entropy loss, ReduceLROnPlateau scheduling, and early stopping. Both tracks are deployed as Gradio applications on Hugging Face Spaces. Source code is publicly available at https://github.com/ikii-sd/pba2026-crazyrichteam.

</details>

### [322] [SwarmDrive: Semantic V2V Coordination for Latency-Constrained Cooperative Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22852)
*Anjie Qiu,Donglin Wang,Zexin Fang,Sanket Partani,Hans D. Schotten*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了SwarmDrive，一种基于语义V2V协作的自动驾驶推理框架，通过本地SLM和高不确定性时的意图分布共享，提升了复杂场景下的驾驶表现，达到了更高成功率和更低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 云端LLM推理带来高延迟且依赖稳定网络，而本地模型在遮挡下表现有限。需要一种兼顾低延迟、高鲁棒性的协作推理方法。

Method: 设计了SwarmDrive框架，车辆本地运行轻量语言模型（SLM），只在高不确定性场合进行车辆间的意图信息共享，结合事件触发一致性融合意图，减少通信开销。并在模拟遮挡路口场景下进行多组对比实验。

Result: 在6G通信假设下，SwarmDrive将成功率从68.9%提升到94.1%，延迟由510ms降到151.4ms。增大协作车辆数会提高通信负载与丢包。最佳表现出现在4台车、熵阈值0.65时，并且协作优势在不同消融实验下依然成立。

Conclusion: 语义V2V边缘协作在特定场景下能在低延迟约束下提升自动驾驶鲁棒性，但该成果尚不等价于对6G系统的真实部署验证。

Abstract: Cloud-hosted LLM inference for autonomous driving adds round-trip delay and depends on stable connectivity, while purely local edge models struggle under occlusion. We present SwarmDrive, a semantic Vehicle-to-Vehicle (V2V) coordination framework in which nearby vehicles run local Small Language Models (SLMs), share compact intent distributions only when uncertainty is high, and fuse them through event-triggered consensus. We evaluate SwarmDrive in a 5-seed executable study built around one occluded intersection case, combining matched operating-point comparisons with robustness sweeps. In that setting, SwarmDrive under its 6G communication setting ("Swarm 6G") raises success from 68.9% to 94.1% over a single local SLM while reducing latency from a 510 ms cloud reference to 151.4 ms. However, an increased number of participating vehicles leads to higher communication overhead and packet loss. SwarmDrive also evaluates the impact of swarm-size, packet-loss, and entropy-threshold sweeps and shows that the cooperative gain holds across ablations and is best balanced near an active swarm size of 4 vehicles and an entropy trigger threshold of 0.65 in the current prototype. These results show that semantic edge cooperation can work under tight latency constraints in the targeted intersection case, but they are not a deployment-grade validation of a real 6G stack.

</details>


### [323] [Airspeed Forward-Invariance for Unpowered Fixed-Wing Aircraft](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22860)
*Huseyin Emre Tekaslan,Ella M. Atkins*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对定翼无人机无动力飞行时空速保护的新方法，通过理论分析和仿真验证，有效保证了在有风情况下飞行器的安全空速范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 定翼无人机在无动力飞行时，空速完全依赖于势能与动能的交换，容易受到飞行引导命令和风的影响，导致空速失控甚至失速。保证在有风情况下执行机动时留在安全空速包络内，是实现无人机自主安全飞行的关键问题。

Method: 作者基于Nagumo切向条件，导出了受风影响下允许飞行轨迹角命令的封闭式条件，确保空速处于安全包络内。进一步，用离线二次规划方法，为不爬升飞行场景设计并验证了安全的机动基元。

Result: 通过高保真无动力定翼机模型仿真，将多个认证安全机动基元拼接，验证了整个滑翔轨迹内空速严格受控于安全包络。

Conclusion: 该方法能保证定翼无人机在稳态风环境下可靠执行安全机动，空速始终处于安全范围。后续将扩展至非稳态风场和实际飞行实验。

Abstract: Autonomous fixed-wing flight is becoming a key capability in aerial robotics, enabling sensing, mobility, and contingency operations across both small-scale Uncrewed Aircraft Systems and large-scale Advanced Air Mobility. During unpowered operation in fixed-wing platforms, airspeed is regulated solely through potential-kinetic energy exchange, making airspeed dynamics highly sensitive to guidance commands, particularly under wind. This paper presents a viability-based airspeed protection for ground-referenced guidance in steady wind, where airspeed evolution depends explicitly on the commanded flight path angle. Leveraging Nagumo's tangency condition, we derive a closed-form, wind-dependent characterization of admissible guidance commands that guarantees forward invariance of a safe airspeed envelope. These conditions are embedded within an offline quadratic programming framework to certify airspeed-safe maneuver primitives for non-ascending flight at the guidance level. The approach is validated using a high-fidelity unpowered fixed-wing aircraft model on gliding trajectories formed by concatenating certified maneuver primitives, demonstrating strict airspeed boundedness. Future work will address unsteady wind fields and flight experiments.

</details>


### [324] [Magnetic Indoor Localization through CNN Regression and Rotation Invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22896)
*Helge Rosé,Konstantin Klipp,Tom Koubek,Bernd Schäufele,Ilja Radusch*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出基于CNN和旋转不变磁场特征的室内定位方法，能有效克服设备方向变化影响，并在多个实际环境中超过现有方法的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于磁场指纹的室内定位方法在遇到设备朝向变化时准确率下降，而实际使用中设备方向难以保持一致，这限制了其应用。本文旨在寻找一种对设备旋转鲁棒的室内定位特征及方法。

Method: 作者提出使用来自3D磁场的两个旋转不变特征（磁场模长Mn和重力轴投影Mg），并设计了轻量级7层扩张卷积神经网络（MagNetS/XL），以端到端方式基于磁场序列回归定位(x, y)。通过MagPie数据集（三栋楼，手持轨迹）在不同旋转条件下系统评估方法性能。

Result: 结果显示，传统3D输入在旋转下定位误差显著增加，而2D旋转不变输入始终保持高精度，并在旋转大于一定阈值后性能优于3D输入。MagNetXL在MagPie数据集上达到甚至超过了最新方法的准确率，MagNetS在参数量大幅减少情况下也表现优异，适合移动端部署。

Conclusion: 本文方法实现了无需额外基础设施、无需朝向校准的高精度室内定位，旋转不变特征大幅提高了定位系统在实际环境下的鲁棒性，适合实际应用推广。

Abstract: Indoor positioning is an essential technology for a wide range of applications in GNSS-denied environments, including indoor navigation and IoT systems. Combining convolutional neural networks (CNNs) and magnetic field-based features offers a low-cost, infrastructure-free solution for precise positioning. While magnetic fingerprints are a promising approach for indoor positioning, models trained on raw 3D magnetometer data are highly sensitive to device orientation. We address this by using two rotation invariant features derived from the 3D magnetic field: the norm (Mn) and the projection onto the gravity axis (Mg). We train a lightweight 7-layer dilated CNN (MagNetS/XL) on magnetic sequences to directly regress (x, y) positions. Using the MagPie dataset (three buildings, handheld trajectories), we systematically evaluate fixed and random rotations of test and/or train data. Raw 3D inputs (Mx, My , Mz) exhibit isotropic error increases under fixed 90° rotations and further degrade with growing random rotations. In contrast, 2D (Mn, Mg) inputs maintain rotation invariant accuracy and surpass the 3D inputs once rotation exceeds building-specific thresholds for three reference buildings: 0° for Loomis (large), 5° for Talbot (medium), and 6° for CSL (small). MagNetXL achieves or exceeds state-of-the-art accuracy on the MagPie dataset, and MagNetS delivers similar performance with roughly one third of the parameters, favoring mobile deployment. These results show that the robustness gained from rotation invariant inputs outweighs the loss of input dimensionality in realistic usage, allowing mapping and localization without orientation alignment or added infrastructure.

</details>


### [325] [RecoverFormer: End-to-End Contact-Aware Recovery for Humanoid Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22911)
*Zihui Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了RECOVERFORMER，一种全端到端的人形机器人恢复策略，能够在不同干扰和环境下实现多模态、自主切换并鲁棒的恢复行为，并在多种扰动和动力学不匹配下验证了其强大的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人形机器人在非结构化环境中的鲁棒恢复能力有限，现有端到端控制策略难以高效处理意外干扰及动态变化，缺乏对多恢复行为的自适应切换和环境交互能力。

Method: 设计了包含因果transformer的网络结构，输入50步历史观测信息，通过两个创新模块：潜在恢复模式头（用于平滑切换多种恢复策略）和接触可行性头（判断环境中助稳表面），无须模式级标注，通过端到端训练获得泛化能力。

Result: 在模拟环境下（MuJoCo，Unitree G1平台），只用开阔地面训练，可零样本迁移到墙面等环境，对100-300N推力和0.25-1.4m墙距实现100%恢复。在各种动力学扰动下表现优异，如+25%质量时恢复率75.5%、30ms延迟89%、低摩擦91.5%、多重扰动99%。

Conclusion: RECOVERFORMER展示了单一端到端策略能够实现多模式、环境感知的人形机器人鲁棒恢复，并能适应各类扰动和环境变化，拥有强泛化和实用潜力。

Abstract: Humanoid robots operating in unstructured environments must recover from unexpected disturbances-a capability that remains challenging for end-to-end control policies. We present RECOVERFORMER, a fully end-to-end humanoid recovery policy that learns when and how to switch among recovery behaviors-including compensatory stepping, hand-environment contact, and center-of-mass reshaping-while maintaining robust performance under model mismatch. The architecture combines a causal transformer over a 50-step observation history with two novel heads: a latent recovery mode that enables smooth transitions among distinct recovery strategies, and a contact affordance head that predicts which environmental surfaces (walls, railings, table edges) are beneficial for stabilization. We evaluate RECOVERFORMER on the Unitree G1 humanoid in MuJoCo. Trained only on open floor, RECOVERFORMER transfers zero shot to walled environments, achieving 100% recovery success across 100-300 N pushes and across wall distances from 0.25-1.4m. Under zero-shot dynamics mismatch, RECOVERFORMER reaches 75.5% at plus +25% mass, 89% under 30 ms latency, 91.5% at low friction, and 99% under compound friction, latency and mass perturbation. The learned latent modes specialize across force regimes without mode-level supervision, validated by t-SNE analysis of 300 episodes. Taken together, these results show that a single end-to-end policy can deliver multi-modal, contact aware humanoid recovery that generalizes across perturbation magnitude, contact geometry, and dynamics shift.

</details>


### [326] [Collaborative Trajectory Prediction via Late Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22973)
*Nadya Abdel Madjid,Murad Mebrahtu,Zakhar Yagudin,Bilal Hassan,Naoufel Werghi,Jorge Dias,Dzmitry Tsetserukou,Majid Khonji*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的协同车辆轨迹预测方法，通过后融合（late-fusion）机制显著降低通信开销，同时提升预测精度，在多个关键数据集上均获得了更好的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的车辆轨迹预测方法在面对遮挡、感知范围有限和感知误差等不确定性时，表现仍不理想。协同V2V方法通过信息共享降低这些不确定性，但现有方法多在感知阶段融合高维特征，造成高通信开销且对带宽等理想化假设依赖强，实际部署受限。

Method: 论文将协同融合从感知阶段转移到预测阶段，采用通用的后融合框架：各车作为异步独立体，分别预测轨迹后，交换和融合预测结果，而不是高维特征。该框架无需模型结构特定假设，适用于不同模型。

Result: 在OPV2V、V2V4Real、DeepAccident等多个数据集上评估，后融合方法在所有数据集上都能显著降低轨迹遗漏率（miss rate），提高0.5米误差下的轨迹成功率（TSR0.5）。在V2V4Real真实场景下，协同预测比独立预测分别提升了1.69%和1.22%的成功率。

Conclusion: 将协同点后移至预测阶段，用结果级的后融合替代特征级通信，可以有效降低协同车辆预测的通信压力，并提升预测准确性，为实际多车协同提供了更实用且高效的解决思路。

Abstract: Predicting future trajectories of surrounding traffic agents is critical for safe autonomous navigation and collision avoidance. Despite all advances in the trajectory forecasting realm, the prediction models remains vulnerable to uncertainty caused by occlusions, limited sensing range, and perception errors. Collaborative vehicle-to-vehicle (V2V) approaches help reduce this uncertainty by sharing complementary information. Existing collaborative trajectory prediction methods typically fuse feature maps at the perception stage to construct a holistic scene view. Further this holistic representation is decoded into the future trajectories. Such design incurs substantial communication overhead due to the exchange of high-dimensional feature representations and often assumes idealized bandwidth and synchronization, limiting practical deployment. We address these limitations by shifting collaboration from perception to the prediction module and introducing a late-fusion framework for shared forecasts. The framework is model-agnostic and treats collaborating vehicles as independent asynchronous agents. We evaluate the approach on the OPV2V, V2V4Real, and DeepAccident datasets, comparing individual and collaborative forecasting. Across all datasets, late fusion consistently reduces miss rate and improves trajectory success rate ($\mathrm{TSR}_{0.5}$), defined as the fraction of ground-truth agents with final displacement error below 0.5 m. On the real-world V2V4Real dataset, collaborative prediction improves the success rate by $1.69\%$ and $1.22\%$ for both intelligent vehicles, respectively, compared with individual forecasting.

</details>


### [327] [Learning from the Best: Smoothness-Driven Metrics for Data Quality in Imitation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23000)
*Soham Kulkarni,Raayan Dhar,Yuchen Cui*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了RINSE框架，通过轨迹平滑性评价行为克隆数据质量，在多个场景中提升了策略性能和数据利用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行为克隆（BC）高度依赖示范数据质量，但现实世界数据往往因操作员技能差异、远程操作失误等导致质量不一，标准BC方法无法区分数据优劣，现有数据筛选方式又依赖高昂的训练成本或人工标注，难以扩展。

Method: RINSE框架基于运动控制理论，认为高质量动作轨迹应更为平滑。RINSE用两种互补指标打分：Spectral Arc Length（SAL），频域的平滑性频谱指标；Trajectory-Envelope Distance（TED），结合接触信号的空间几何偏差指标。它完全基于轨迹数据，泛用性强，无需深入模型或人工参与。

Result: SAL过滤可只用六分之一的数据获得16%的性能提升。TED过滤在实际操作中用一半数据提升20%。与STRAP结合进行重排序可使平均成功率提升5.6%。在Re-Mix域权重分配中，RINSE得分与学习型分配结果高度相关（Spearman ρ≥0.89）。

Conclusion: 轨迹平滑度可作为行为克隆等决策任务中高效的数据质量信号，在噪声高或异质性数据下，对筛选、检索、重加权均有显著提升作用。

Abstract: In behavioral cloning (BC), policy performance is fundamentally limited by demonstration data quality. Real-world datasets contain trajectories of varying quality due to operator skill differences, teleoperation artifacts, and procedural inconsistencies, yet standard BC treats all demonstrations equally. Existing curation methods require costly policy training in the loop or manual annotation, limiting scalability. We propose RINSE (Ranking and INdexing Smooth Examples), a lightweight framework for scoring demonstrations based on trajectory smoothness that is policy-architecture-agnostic and operates on trajectory data alone, with TED additionally using a phase-boundary/contact signal. Grounded in motor control theory, which establishes smoothness as a hallmark of skilled movement, RINSE uses two complementary metrics: Spectral Arc Length (SAL), a spectral measure of frequency-domain regularity, and Trajectory-Envelope Distance (TED), a spatial measure of contact-aware geometric deviation. We show that smoothness filtering can reduce the conditional action variance of the retained data distribution, with downstream effects that can be amplified by action chunking and compounding error. On RoboMimic benchmarks, SAL filtering achieves 16% higher success using one-sixth of the data. On real-world manipulation, TED filtering achieves 20% improvement with half the data. As a retrieval-stage filter within STRAP on LIBERO-10, RINSE re-ranking improves mean success by 5.6%. As soft weights in Re-Mix domain reweighting, RINSE scores produce domain allocations highly correlated with the learned Re-Mix allocations (Spearman $ρ\geq 0.89$). These results support smoothness as a useful quality signal across filtering, retrieval, and reweighting settings, especially in noisy or heterogeneous data regimes.

Method: 文章从数据集、基准测试、数据引擎三大支柱梳理VLA领域，分析了数据集类型与构成、基准任务复杂性与结构、数据引擎的类别及局限。通过结构化分析，总结当前主要的问题与障碍。

Abstract: Despite remarkable progress in Vision--Language--Action (VLA) models, a central bottleneck remains underexamined: the data infrastructure that underlies embodied learning. To this end, we present a systematic, data-centric analysis of VLA research organized around three pillars: datasets, benchmarks, and data engines. For datasets, we categorize real-world and synthetic corpora along embodiment diversity, modality composition, and action space formulation, revealing a persistent fidelity-cost trade-off that fundamentally constrains large-scale collection. For benchmarks, we analyze task complexity and environment structure jointly, exposing structural gaps in compositional generalization and long-horizon reasoning evaluation that existing protocols fail to address. For data engines, we examine simulation-based, video-reconstruction, and automated task-generation paradigms, identifying their shared limitations in physical grounding and sim-to-real transfer. ### [329] [Equivariant Filter for Radar-Inertial Odometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23033)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于EKF的雷达-惯性测程对雷达和IMU间的高精度外参数标定依赖很大，并且对扰动很敏感，线性化误差较大会导致性能下降甚至滤波发散，亟需更鲁棒且一致性有保障的状态估计方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于李群对称性的等变滤波器，将导航状态和IMU零偏几何耦合，并扩展以包含雷达-IMU外参数标定与多状态约束更新，从理论结构实现滤波器一致性。

Result: 在两种不同无人机上进行了真实实验，EqF-RIO在外参数标定准确时达到了最先进的精度，在校准误差较大的情况下也能很好地收敛，而传统EKF-RIO则失败。同时开源了评测代码。

Conclusion: 该方法本质上提升了系统鲁棒性和一致性，使状态估计器即使在极差的初始化条件下依然可靠，优于现有传统滤波方法。

Abstract: Radar-Inertial Odometry (RIO) based on the Extended Kalman Filter (EKF) relies on accurate extrinsic calibration between the radar and the Inertial Measurement Unit (IMU) and is sensitive to disturbances, as large linearization errors can degrade performance or even cause divergence. To address these limitations, this letter proposes an Equivariant Filter (EqF) for RIO based on a Lie group symmetry that geometrically couples navigation states and IMU biases, extending it to incorporate radar-IMU extrinsic calibration and multi-state constraint updates. This equivariant formulation inherently preserves consistency and enhances robustness, enabling reliable state estimation even under poor or completely wrong initialization of calibration states. Real-world experiments on two different Uncrewed Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) show that the proposed EqF-RIO achieves state-of-the-art accuracy under correct extrinsic calibration and offers improved convergence under large calibration errors, where the conventional EKF-RIO fails. Evaluation code is open-sourced.

*Rui Luo,Jonas Mariager Jakobsen,Wesley Roozing,Federico Califano,Cheng Fang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理人机交互系统中，安全性是部署的核心挑战；现有CBF虽能实现安全，但面对多任务和冲突时灵活性有限。

Method: 结合CBF与分层二次规划（HQP），将安全任务和性能任务分层嵌入，允许任务之间有层级关系，在柔性冲突情况下能确保至少高优先级安全任务被满足。

In recent years, Control Barrier Function (CBF) has emerged as an effective approach to enforce safety guarantees, which has been widely applied in various applications, from adaptive cruise control to navigation of legged robots. CBFs can be solved in a Quadratic Programming (QP) problem, which can include many CBF-formulated tasks. To manage a large number of safety tasks, a hierarchical CBF has been used to allow hierarchical relaxation of safety tasks to ensure the feasibility of a solution in the presence of conflicting tasks. In this work, we propose to use a CBF-based Hierarchical Quadratic Programming (HQP) framework in physical human-robot interaction to allow us to design both performance tasks (e.g., preserve the desired behavior at the human-robot interaction point) and safety tasks at any level of a hierarchy to balance the safety and the performance in a more flexible way. Extensive experiments were carried out on a real redundant robot to validate the effectiveness, flexibility, and generality of this approach.

### [332] [Breaking Lock-In: Preserving Steerability under Low-Data VLA Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23121)
*Suning Huang,Jiaqi Shao,Ke Wang,Qianzhong Chen,Jiankai Sun,Yanjiang Guo,Mac Schwager,Jeannette Bohg*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文发现常用的少量示范微调（SFT）会导致通用视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型响应新指令能力下降，即“锁定现象”。提出新方法DeLock，只需结合模型原有知识与测试时对比引导提示，即可缓解锁定，提升泛化，无需更多辅助数据。实验证明DeLock优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者发现用少量数据对通用VLA模型进行微调，会使模型过拟合于新数据，难以泛化给新任务和新指令，即出现“锁定”现象。这严重限制了VLA模型在实际场景下的通用性和适应性。

Method: 提出DeLock方法：在后续微调过程中保持模型原有的视觉基础，同时在测试阶段用对比提升的引导提示（contrastive prompt guidance）来引导模型在新指令下恢复泛化能力，利用原有的预训练知识，无需额外的监督信号或大规模新数据。

Result: 在8个模拟和真实世界任务中，DeLock均显著优于当前主流方法，且其性能与用大量人工示范数据微调的最先进通用策略持平或更佳。

Conclusion: DeLock充分利用已预训练模型中的知识，通过简单的机制恢复泛化能力，无需大幅增加标注数据或引入复杂的辅助损失，能有效解决VLA模型微调时的锁定问题。

Abstract: Have you ever post-trained a generalist vision-language-action (VLA) policy on a small demonstration dataset, only to find that it stops responding to new instructions and is limited to behaviors observed during post-training? We identify this phenomenon as lock-in: after low-data, supervised fine-tuning (SFT), the policy becomes overly specialized to the post-training data and fails to generalize to novel instructions, manifesting as concept lock-in (fixation on training objects/attributes) and spatial lock-in (fixation on training spatial targets). Many existing remedies introduce additional supervision signals, such as those derived from foundation models or auxiliary objectives, or rely on augmented datasets to recover generalization. In this paper, we show that the policy's internal pre-trained knowledge is sufficient: DeLock mitigates lock-in by preserving visual grounding during post-training and applying test-time contrastive prompt guidance to steer the policy's denoising dynamics according to novel instructions. Across eight simulation and real-world evaluations, DeLock consistently outperforms strong baselines and matches or exceeds the performance of a state-of-the-art generalist policy post-trained with substantially more curated demonstrations.

### [334] [BridgeACT: Bridging Human Demonstrations to Robot Actions via Unified Tool-Target Affordances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23249)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: BridgeACT将操作任务分为“抓取位置”和“移动方式”两个阶段。先从场景中定位任务相关的可供性区域，再从人类演示预测任务相关的3D运动可供性。最后，这些可供性通过抓取模块和闭环运动控制器转化为机器人的具体动作，无需机器人演示数据。同时，把复杂任务分解为多个可供性操作，统一处理多样任务和不同对象间交互。

Result: 在真实机器人抓取和操作实验中，BridgeACT相较于之前的方法表现更优，并且对新物体、新场景和新视角表现出更强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: BridgeACT方法实现了不依赖机器人演示的机器人操作任务学习，大幅提升了模型的泛化性与可部署性，为从人类视频端到端学习机器人操作提供了新范式。

Abstract: Learning robot manipulation from human videos is appealing due to the scale and diversity of human demonstrations, but transferring such demonstrations to executable robot behavior remains challenging. Prior work either relies on robot data for downstream adaptation or learns affordance representations that remain at the perception level and do not directly support real-world execution. We present BridgeACT, an affordance-driven framework that learns robotic manipulation directly from human videos without requiring any robot demonstration data. Our key idea is to model affordance as an embodiment-agnostic intermediate representation that bridges human demonstrations and robot actions. BridgeACT decomposes manipulation into two complementary problems: where to grasp and how to move. To this end, BridgeACT first grounds task-relevant affordance regions in the current scene, and then predicts task-conditioned 3D motion affordances from human demonstrations. The resulting affordances are mapped to robot actions through a grasping module and a lightweight closed-loop motion controller, enabling direct deployment on real robots. In addition, we represent complex manipulation tasks as compositions of affordance operations, which allows a unified treatment of diverse tasks and object-to-object interactions. Experiments on real-world manipulation tasks show that BridgeACT outperforms prior baselines and generalizes to unseen objects, scenes, and viewpoints.

In this paper, we propose MoSS, a modular sensory stream framework that adapts VLAs to leverage multiple sensory signals for action prediction. Specifically, we introduce decoupled modality streams that integrate heterogeneous physical signals into the action stream via joint cross-modal self-attention. Furthermore, to better capture contact interaction dynamics, we incorporate an auxiliary task that predicts future physical signals. ### [336] [An Efficient Beam Search Algorithm for Active Perception in Mobile Robotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23327)
*Kaixian Qu,Han Wang,Victor Klemm,Cesar Cadena,Marco Hutter*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套新的主动感知路径规划方法，结合了节点级束搜索（NBS）、期望增益评估指标和快速探索随机环形图（RRAG）三项创新，显著提高了信息采集效率，并在实际机器人平台上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主动感知任务面临两难：传统的旅行商算法虽然可找到高质量路径，但计算开销大；最短路径树方法虽然高效，却受限过多，影响信息收集质量。急需兼顾效率与效果的中间产品。

Method: 1. 提出节点级束搜索(NBS)，为每个节点维护top-B候选，克服标准束搜索容易陷入局部最优的问题；2. 在路径选择标准中引入前沿与期望增益，提升探索-利用之间的平衡；3. 提出快速探索随机环形图（RRAG），用于复杂环境下的图生成和连通性保障。

Result: NBS在多个基准图中，相比其他基础方法，在束宽很低时依旧表现优秀；NBS和RRAG结合后在三类主动感知任务上全部取得最优，部分任务超越现有SOTA方法20%以上，且在真实机器人平台上实验验证了其实用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 作者提出的方法兼具高效率和高质量，能更好地指导机器人进行主动感知任务，为实际复杂环境中的路径规划问题提供了可行和优越的解决思路，对机器人感知领域有重要推动作用。

Abstract: Active perception is a fundamental problem in autonomous robotics in which the robot must decide where to move and what to sense in order to obtain the most informative observations for accomplishing its mission. Existing approaches either solve a computationally expensive traveling salesman problem over heuristically selected informative nodes, or adopt a more efficient but overly constrained shortest path tree formulation. To address these limitations, we explore beam search algorithms as scalable alternatives. While the standard beam search provides scalability by preserving the top-B paths at each depth level, it is prone to local optima and exhibits parameter sensitivity. Our first contribution is a node-wise beam search (NBS) algorithm, which maintains top-B candidates per node to enable more effective exploration of the solution space. Systematic benchmarking on graphs shows that NBS consistently outperforms other baselines and maintains strong performance even at low beam widths. As a second contribution, we integrate the concept of frontiers into the path selection criterion, introducing the expected gain metric, which better balances exploration and exploitation compared to existing alternatives. Our third contribution proposes the rapidly-exploring random annulus graph (RRAG), a novel graph construction method that preserves full orientation sampling and ensures connectivity in cluttered environments through a fallback local sampling-based planner. Extensive experiments demonstrate that NBS combined with RRAG achieves the highest performance across all three representative active perception tasks, outperforming state-of-the-art algorithms by at least 20% in one or more tasks. We further validate the approach on real robotic platforms in different scenarios.

</details>


### [337] [Learning from Demonstration with Failure Awareness for Safe Robot Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23360)
*Xianghui Wang,Siwei Cheng,Shanze Wang,Xinming Zhang,Dan Zhang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向失败体验的机器人导航学习方法，通过将失败数据与成功演示解耦，提高了导航的安全性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器人示范学习主要利用成功的演示数据，导致对不安全状态覆盖不足，机器人遇到未见过情形时容易发生碰撞。失败经验虽富含不安全区的信息，但直接用于策略学习却会导致性能下降，因此需要一种新方式使其有效利用。

Method: 提出了一种失败感知学习框架，将失败数据用于危险区域的价值估计，仅用成功演示进行策略学习，在离线强化学习环境中实现，并通过仿真和真实世界测试。

Result: 实验显示，该方法在各种环境及机器人平台下均能有效减少碰撞率，同时保持较高的任务成功率，并具备良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过将失败和成功数据分工使用，可以充分利用失败经验提升导航安全性而不损害行为性能，为机器人导航学习提供了更可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Learning from demonstration is widely used for robot navigation, yet it suffers from a fundamental limitation: demonstrations consist predominantly of successful behaviors and provide limited coverage of unsafe states. This limitation leads to poor safety when the robot encounters scenarios beyond the demonstration distribution. Failure experiences, such as collisions, contain essential information about unsafe regions, but remain underutilized. The key difficulty lies in the fact that failure data do not provide valid guidance for action imitation, and their naive incorporation into policy learning often degrades performance. We address this challenge by proposing a failure-aware learning framework that explicitly decouples the roles of success and failure data. In this framework, failure experiences are used to shape value estimation in hazardous regions, while policy learning is restricted to successful demonstrations. This separation enables the effective use of failure data without corrupting policy behavior. We implement this design within an offline reinforcement learning (RL) setting and evaluate it in both simulation and real-world environments. The results show that our framework consistently reduces collision rates while preserving the task success rate, and demonstrate strong generalization across different environments and robot platforms.

</details>


### [338] [Large Language Model based Interactive Decision-Making for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23513)
*Xinwei Dong,Jiyang Li,Jiabin Xie,Yang Yi,Tianshang Jia,Shiyu Fang,Ye Tian,Peng Hang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动驾驶系统在高冲突、人机混合交通情境中过于保守，缺乏主动交互，导致公众接受度不高。为减少意图误解和决策失误，需要更加智能且具有良好人机互动的决策方法。

Method: （1）用对象-过程方法（OPM）对多车场景进行语义建模；（2）大语言模型解析环境中各主体的显式与隐式意图，并在安全与效率约束下选取候选动作；（3）通过蒙特卡洛采样生成轨迹，选取最优可执行方案；（4）最终决策转化为简明自然语言消息，通过eHMI对外发布，形成理解-行动-沟通闭环。

Result: 在群体驾驶仿真器实验中，该方法在安全、舒适和效率指标上均优于传统基线方法。类似图灵测试的评估显示，决策高度拟人化。

To mitigate intent misunderstandings and decision failures, we present a Large Language Model based interactive decision-making framework that augments scene understanding and intent-aware interaction to jointly improve safety and efficiency. The approach uses Object-Process Methodology to semantically model complex multi-vehicle scenes, abstracting low-level perceptual data into objects, processes, and relations, thereby streamlining reasoning over latent causal structure. Building on this representation, the Large Language Model parses both explicit and implicit intents of surrounding agents and, under jointly enforced safety and efficiency constraints, selects candidate maneuvers. We further generate perturbed trajectory candidates via Monte Carlo sampling and evaluate them to obtain an optimized executable trajectory. To foster transparency and coordination with nearby road users, the final decision is translated by the Large Language Model into concise natural-language messages and broadcast through an external Human-Machine Interface, completing a closed loop from scene understanding to action to language. Experiments in a cluster driving simulator demonstrate that the proposed method outperforms traditional baselines across safety, comfort, and efficiency metrics, while a Turing-test-style evaluation indicates a high degree of human-likeness in decision making. Besides, these results suggest that coupling semantic scene abstraction with Large Language Model mediated intent reasoning and language-based eHMI communication offers a practical pathway toward interactive, trustworthy autonomous driving in dense mixed traffic.

As such, we present EgoLive, a large-scale, high-quality egocentric dataset designed explicitly for robot manipulation learning. EgoLive establishes three distinctive technical advantages over existing egocentric datasets: first, it represents the largest open-source annotated egocentric dataset focused on real-world task-oriented human routines to date; second, it delivers leading data quality via a customized head-mounted capture device and comprehensive high-precision multi-modal annotations; third, all data is collected exclusively in unconstrained real-world scenarios and encompasses vertical field human working data, including home service, retail, and other practical work scenarios, providing superior diversity and ecological validity. While large language models (LLMs) excel at general code generation, they struggle with the semantic gap between physical descriptions and simulation implementation. We introduce PhysCodeBench, the first comprehensive benchmark for evaluating physics-aware symbolic simulation, comprising 700 manually-crafted diverse samples across mechanics, fluid dynamics, and soft-body physics with expert annotations. Our evaluation framework measures both code executability and physical accuracy through automated and visual assessment. Building on this, we propose a Self-Corrective Multi-Agent Refinement Framework (SMRF) with three specialized agents (simulation generator, error corrector, and simulation refiner) that collaborate iteratively with domain-specific validation to produce physically accurate simulations. SMRF achieves 67.7 points overall performance compared to 36.3 points for the best baseline among evaluated SOTA models, representing a 31.4-point improvement. Our analysis demonstrates that error correction is critical for accurate physics-aware symbolic simulation and that specialized multi-agent approaches significantly outperform single-agent methods across the tested physical domains.

### [341] [Tube Diffusion Policy: Reactive Visual-Tactile Policy Learning for Contact-rich Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23609)
*Teng Xue,Alberto Rigo,Bingjian Huang,Jiayi Shen,Zhengtong Xu,Nick Colonnese,Amirhossein H. Memar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种名为Tube Diffusion Policy (TDP)的新型模仿学习框架，可通过视觉和触觉反馈，实现具备高反应性和自适应能力的接触丰富操作。与现有方法相比，TDP在多项基准任务和实际实验中表现更优，尤其适合实时高频反馈控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模仿学习在接触丰富操作中，常通过动作分组（chunking）实现动作生成，这导致对突发情况和高频触觉信号的反应不够灵活和即时。为更好实现操作中的快速自适应与高反应性控制，亟需一种能融合多模态感知且支持实时反馈的新方法。

Method: 作者提出Tube Diffusion Policy (TDP)框架，将扩散模型的模仿学习与基于tube的反馈控制相结合。核心做法是：在名义动作序列周围学习一个“动作tube”，使得策略在执行时能根据实时视觉和触觉观测快速纠正轨迹，实现连续、高效的反馈流。TDP能大幅减少扩散模型所需的降噪步骤，加快控制响应速度。

Result: 在Push-T基准和另外三项复杂的视觉-触觉操作任务中，TDP均优于现有最先进的模仿学习模型。两个真实世界实验进一步证明了TDP在面对接触不确定性和外部干扰时的高鲁棒性和响应能力。

Conclusion: TDP有效结合生成模型和反馈控制，实现了具备高鲁棒性、高反应性和强自适应能力的接触操作新范式。通过减少降噪步骤，TDP非常适用于需要实时高频反馈的高难度操作机器人场景。

Abstract: Contact-rich manipulation is central to many everyday human activities, requiring continuous adaptation to contact uncertainty and external disturbances through multi-modal perception, particularly vision and tactile feedback. While imitation learning has shown strong potential for learning complex manipulation behaviors, most existing approaches rely on action chunking, which fundamentally limits their ability to react to unforeseen observations during execution. This limitation becomes especially critical in contact-rich scenarios, where physical uncertainty and high-frequency tactile feedback demand rapid, reactive control. To address this challenge, we propose Tube Diffusion Policy (TDP), a novel reactive visual-tactile policy learning framework that bridges diffusion-based imitation learning with tube-based feedback control. By leveraging the expressive power of generative models, TDP learns an observation-conditioned feedback flow around nominal action chunks, forming an action tube that enables fast and adaptive reactions during execution. We evaluate TDP on the widely used Push-T benchmark and three additional challenging visual-tactile dexterous manipulation tasks. Across all benchmarks, TDP consistently outperforms state-of-the-art imitation learning baselines. Two real-world experiments further validate its robust reactivity under contact uncertainty and external disturbances. Moreover, the step-wise correction mechanism enabled by action tube significantly reduces the required denoising steps, making TDP well suited for real-time, high-frequency feedback control in contact-rich manipulation.

*Haoming Xu,Lei Lei,Jie Gu,Chu Tang,Jingmin Chen,Ruiqi Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的视觉-语言动作框架Move-Then-Operate，通过将机械臂操作分为“移动”和“操作”两个阶段，提高了高精度操作任务的成功率和学习效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人操控方法常常将不同类型的行为混为一体，导致学习过程低效，尤其是在高精度操作任务中难以取得理想效果。作者希望通过分阶方法，模拟人类运动规律，提升操作表现。

Method: 该方法将操作过程分为“移动”阶段和“操作”阶段，通过具备可学习能力的阶段选择器进行切换，每一阶段由专门的策略专家掌控。阶段标签通过MLLM（多模态大模型）自动生成，结合上下文提示（如末端执行器速度、任务分解）以贴合人类运动习惯。

Result: 在RoboTwin2基准测试中，该方法平均成功率达68.9%，相较于基线方法提升24%，在数据使用量减少10倍以及训练步骤减少40%的情况下仍达到或超过SOTA表现。

Conclusion: 将复杂操控任务结构化拆解后，显著提升了学习效率和操作性能，为高精度机器人操控提供了有效解决思路。

Abstract: We present Move-Then-Operate, a Vision language action framework that explicitly decouples robotic manipulation into two distinct behavioral phases: coarse relocation (move) and contact-critical interaction (operate). Unlike monolithic policies that conflate these heterogeneous regimes, our architecture employs a dual-expert policy routed by a learnable phase selector, introducing a structural inductive bias that isolates phase-specific dynamics. Phase labels are automatically generated via an MLLM-based pipeline conditioned on lightweight contextual cues such as end-effector velocity and subtask decomposition to ensure alignment with human motor patterns. Evaluated on the RoboTwin2 benchmark, our method achieves an average success rate of $68.9\%$, outperforming the monolithic $π_0$ baseline by $24\%$. It matches or exceeds models trained on $10\times$ more data and reaches peak performance in $40\%$ fewer training steps, demonstrating that architectural disentanglement of move and operate phases is a highly effective and efficient strategy for mastering high-precision manipulation.

### [343] [Safe Navigation in Unknown and Cluttered Environments via Direction-Aware Convex Free-Region Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23648)
*Zhicheng Song,Yongjian Li,Kai Chen,Yulin Li,Fan Shi,Jun Ma*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的导航框架，能够针对拥挤环境中的机器人导航，高效生成更适合机器人运动的凸无碰撞区域，并通过连续安全的轨迹生成方法保障机器人的连续无碰撞运动。实验验证了方法在2D、3D及现实场景下的有效性和适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于凸自由区域的规划方法在复杂和拥挤环境下，往往无法生成既能容纳机器人几何尺寸又有利于机器人下游运动的区域，特别是在狭窄通道中易受限制。此外，离散采样下的安全性检查并不能保证实际轨迹的连续无碰撞性，尤其对精细化的机器人几何模型而言，存在安全隐患。

Method: 提出将候选运动方向和机器人几何特性共同纳入到凸自由区生成过程中，使生成的区域兼具空间利用率和运动延展性。同时，结合Lipschitz连续性理论，实现对轨迹的连续安全性认证与局部优化。所有自由区及运动方向被维护在一个基于区域的图中，支持递增式路径规划。该方法在模拟和实物平台上（如四足机器人、无人机）进行了验证。

Result: 在2D杂乱场景下，所提方法生成的凸自由区更加贴合机器人下游可行运动，能够提升整体导航可靠性和安全性，并在三维和实际硬件实验中表现出良好的扩展性和实用性。

Conclusion: 该框架能够解决现有自由区方法在复杂环境下的局限，实现面向机器人几何和运动方向的凸自由区生成，为下游连续安全运动提供了理论和工程保障，具有较高的推广和应用价值。

Abstract: Convex free regions provide a structured and optimization-friendly representation of collision-free space for robot navigation in unknown and cluttered environments. However, existing methods typically enlarge local collision-free regions mainly according to surrounding obstacle geometry. In cluttered environments, such strategies may fail to generate regions that both accommodate robot geometry and preserve traversable extension along candidate motion directions, thereby limiting downstream traversal, especially in narrow passages. Even when such a region is available, safe motion generation remains challenging, because safety checking at discretized trajectory samples does not guarantee continuously collision-free motion when robot geometry is modeled explicitly. To address these issues, we propose a navigation framework that jointly incorporates candidate motion directions and robot geometry into convex free-region generation, and achieves continuously collision-free motion through continuous-safe trajectory generation. Within each region, the framework performs geometry-aware target pose selection and trajectory generation, together with Lipschitz-based continuous safety certification and local refinement. The resulting free regions and candidate motions are maintained in a region-based graph to support incremental planning. Quantitative results in cluttered 2D navigation scenarios show that the proposed method generates free regions better aligned with downstream traversal and enables reliable collision-free navigation, while additional 3D and real-world experiments on a quadrupedal robot and a UAV demonstrate the extensibility and practical applicability of the framework. The open-source project can be found at https://github.com/ZhichengSong6/FRGraph.

</details>


### [344] [Decentralized Heterogeneous Multi-Robot Collaborative Exploration for Indoor and Outdoor 3D Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23693)
*Yuxiang Li,Kun Chen,Jiancheng Wang,Shihao Fang,Haoyao Chen,Yunhui Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种去中心化的异构多机器人协作框架，实现3D环境下的自主探索，提高探索效率与通信节约。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂环境下，异构多机器人系统具备良好的适应性，但如何高效协同以充分发挥各自潜力仍是核心难题。

Method: 设计了融合地形与观测指标的感知地图，引入改进的超体素分割以简化地图结构。通过对机器人可穿越性和可观测性建模，分组和聚类探索任务视角，将任务分配建模为带有约束的异构多出发点多旅行商问题，并采用改进遗传算法求解，优化分配、消除冗余视角、解决运动路径冲突。

Result: 在复杂室内外环境的仿真和实地实验中，与同类先进方法相比，所提方法在探索效率和通信节约方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 该去中心化协作框架能够高效协调异构多机器人在复杂环境中的自主探索，提升系统整体性能，验证了其实用价值。

Abstract: Heterogeneous multi-robot systems feature significant adaptability for complex environments. However, effective collaboration that fully exploits the robots' potential remains a core challenge. This paper proposes a decentralized collaborative framework for heterogeneous multi-robot systems to autonomously explore indoor and outdoor 3D environments. First, a basic perception map that integrates terrain and observation metrics is designed. Improved supervoxel segmentation is developed to simplify the map structure and form a high-level representation that supports lightweight communication. Second, the traversal and observation capabilities of heterogeneous robots are modeled to evaluate the requirements of task views derived from incomplete supervoxels. These task views are grouped by requirements and clustered to streamline assignment. Subsequently, the view-cluster assignment is formulated as a heterogeneous multi-depot multi-traveling salesman problem (HMDMTSP) that incorporates constraints between view-cluster requirements and robot capabilities. An improved genetic algorithm is developed to efficiently solve this problem while ensuring global consistency. Based on the assignments, redundant views within clusters are eliminated to refine exploration routes. Finally, conflicts between robots' motion paths are resolved. Simulations and field experiments in cluttered indoor and outdoor environments demonstrate that our approach effectively coordinates exploration tasks among heterogeneous robots, achieving superior exploration efficiency and communication savings compared to state-of-the-art approaches.

</details>


### [345] [Real-Time Non-Contact Force Compensation for Wrist-Mounted Force/Torque Sensors in Haptic-Enabled Robotic Surgery Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23696)
*Walid Shaker,Mustafa Suphi Erden*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于递归最小二乘法的实时补偿方法，用于低成本机器人辅助手术训练中手腕安装F/T传感器的非接触力矩补偿，实现了高精度触觉反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前高性能触觉反馈系统价格昂贵，限制了其在训练与研究中的普及。需要开发低成本且可靠的触觉反馈方案。

Method: 将F/T传感器安装在机器人手腕，实现触觉反馈功能。针对手腕安装带来的非接触力（如重力、偏置等）影响，设计了基于递归最小二乘法的补偿算法，无需频繁标定，适应环境变化。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在非接触力的补偿误差降低超95%，在非接触力矩的补偿误差降低超91%，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 所提方法能有效提升低成本机器人手术训练装置的触觉反馈准确性，具备现实应用潜力，有望推动机器人手术培训与研究的发展。

Abstract: Haptic feedback has been a long-missed feature in robotic-assisted surgery, one that would allow surgeons to perceive tissue properties and apply controlled forces during delicate procedures. Although commercial robotic systems have begun to integrate haptic technologies, their high costs limit accessibility for training and research purposes. To address this gap, we extend our previously developed low-cost robotic surgery training setup, RoboScope, by incorporating a wrist-mounted force/torque (F/T) sensor for haptic feedback training. Wrist-mounted sensing avoids many challenges associated with tip-mounted sensors but introduces additional non-contact forces, such as gravity, sensor bias, installation offsets, and associated torques, which compromise measurement accuracy. In this paper, we propose a robust real-time compensation method based on recursive least squares (RLS). This method eliminates the need for dataset collection and frequent recalibration while adapting to changing operating conditions. Experimental validation demonstrates that the proposed approach achieves over 95% error reduction in non-contact force compensation and more than 91% in non-contact torque compensation, significantly outperforming existing methods. These results highlight the potential of our approach for providing reliable haptic feedback in robotic surgery training and research.

</details>


### [346] [QuietWalk: Physics-Informed Reinforcement Learning for Ground Reaction Force-Aware Humanoid Locomotion Under Diverse Footwear](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23702)
*Hanze Hu,Luying Feng,Silu Chen,Tianjiang Zheng,Dexin Jiang,Wei Chen,Chi Zhang,Guilin Yang,Yaochu Jin*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理启发和强化学习的安静行走框架QuietWalk，使类人机器人在不同鞋类和地面条件下能显著减弱落地冲击、降低振动和噪音，无需部署端力传感器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人安静行走控制依赖于运动学代理目标或易损的力传感器，而鞋类变化带来的接触力分布变化，会影响已有策略的泛化能力，因此亟需鲁棒、传感友好的方法。

Method: 提出QuietWalk框架，利用受逆动力学约束的物理启发神经网络（PINN）从机器人自身感知推测每只脚的垂直地反力，将预测模型集成进强化学习训练，通过惩罚估测冲击力实现低噪音行走，无需实际力传感器参与部署。

Result: 在真实机器人数据集上，相比完全监督学习预测，逆动力学一致性优化使地反力预测误差降低82%-86%，determination系数显著提高。实物机器人测试下，行走噪声平均降低超7dB，峰值降低近5dB。不同鞋类和多表面测试也展现出较强泛化和适应性。

Conclusion: QuietWalk在无需额外硬件传感器的前提下，有效提升了类人机器人在多样鞋类、地面上的低噪稳健行走表现，有助于改善用户体验并延长硬件寿命。

Abstract: Humanoid robots operating in human-centered environments (e.g., homes, hospitals, and offices) must mitigate foot--ground impact transients, as impact-induced vibration and noise degrade user experience and repeated impacts accelerate hardware wear. However, existing low-noise locomotion training often relies on kinematic proxy objectives or fragile force sensors, and footwear-induced changes in contact dynamics introduce distribution shifts that hinder policy generalization.We present QuietWalk, a physics-informed reinforcement learning framework for ground-reaction-force-aware humanoid locomotion under diverse footwear conditions. QuietWalk employs an inverse-dynamics-constrained physics-informed neural network (PINN) to estimate per-foot vertical ground reaction forces (GRFs) from proprioceptive signals, and integrates the frozen predictor into the RL training loop to penalize predicted impact forces without requiring force sensors at deployment.On a held-out real-robot dataset, enforcing inverse-dynamics consistency reduces vertical GRF prediction errors by 82%-86% compared with a purely supervised predictor and improves the coefficient of determination from 0.39/0.67 to 0.99/0.99 for the left/right feet. On hardware at 1.2 m/s (barefoot; averaged over four floor materials), QuietWalk reduces mean A-weighted noise level by 7.17 dB and peak noise level by 4.98 dB under a consistent recording setup. Cross-footwear experiments (barefoot, skate shoes, athletic sneakers, and high heels) across multiple surfaces further demonstrate robust adaptation to footwear-induced contact variations.

</details>

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are emerging as a unified substrate for embodied intelligence. This shift raises a new class of safety challenges, stemming from the embodied nature of VLA systems, including irreversible physical consequences, a multimodal attack surface across vision, language, and state, real-time latency constraints on defense, error propagation over long-horizon trajectories, and vulnerabilities in the data supply chain. Yet the literature remains fragmented across robotic learning, adversarial machine learning, AI alignment, and autonomous systems safety. This survey provides a unified and up-to-date overview of safety in Vision-Language-Action models. We organize the field along two parallel timing axes, attack timing (training-time vs. inference-time and defense timing (training-time vs. inference-time, linking each class of threat to the stage at which it can be mitigated. We first define the scope of VLA safety, distinguishing it from text-only LLM safety and classical robotic safety, and review the foundations of VLA models, including architectures, training paradigms, and inference mechanisms. We then examine the literature through four lenses: Attacks, Defenses, Evaluation, and Deployment. We survey training-time threats such as data poisoning and backdoors, as well as inference-time attacks including adversarial patches, cross-modal perturbations, semantic jailbreaks, and freezing attacks. We review training-time and runtime defenses, analyze existing benchmarks and metrics, and discuss safety challenges across six deployment domains. Finally, we highlight key open problems, including certified robustness for embodied trajectories, physically realizable defenses, safety-aware training, unified runtime safety architectures, and standardized evaluation.

### [349] [Cooptimizing Safety and Performance Using Safety Value-Constrained Model Predictive Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23863)
*Hao Wang,Nam Nguyen,Armand Jordana,Ludovic Righetti,Somil Bansal*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文针对自主系统在需满足状态和输入约束下的安全性问题，提出在MPC终端约束中引入基于安全值函数的方法，实现了更高的性能与可验证的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MPC在有限时域外的安全性难以保证，现有方法多依赖于局部线性化或保守近似，难以兼顾安全性与性能。

Method: 通过在MPC每一个规划终点引入基于可达性分析的安全值函数约束，确保系统进入控制不变的安全集，实现实时、安全、高性能的轨迹规划。该方法采用可达性安全值函数替代传统的终端集近似，使约束不仅不保守，还能更广泛表达安全性。

Result: 在Flexiv Rizon 10s机械臂仿真和硬件实验验证中，新框架在约束满足性和鲁棒性方面均优于标准MPC和反应式安全过滤器，同时任务性能可比传统方案。全部代码与实验已开源。

Conclusion: 基于可达性安全值函数的MPC终端约束能确保持续安全且具有较高约束满足率与鲁棒性，相比传统保守近似能提供更强的表达力与性能保障。

Abstract: Autonomous systems are increasingly deployed in real-world environments, where they must achieve high performance while maintaining safety under state and input constraints. Although Model Predictive Control (MPC) provides a principled framework for constrained optimal control, guaranteeing safety beyond its finite planning horizon remains a fundamental challenge. In this work, we augment MPC with a safety value function-based terminal constraint that enforces membership in a control-invariant safe set at the end of each planning horizon. This formulation enables real-time synthesis of trajectories that are both high-performing and provably safe. We show that, under an exact safety value function and a feasible initialization, the proposed MPC scheme is recursively feasible, thereby ensuring persistent safety. In contrast to traditional terminal set constructions that rely on local linearizations or conservative approximations, our approach incorporates a reachability-based safety value function for terminal constraints, yielding less conservative and more expressive safety guarantees. We validate the proposed framework through simulation and hardware experiments on a Flexiv Rizon 10s manipulator. Results demonstrate improved constraint satisfaction and robustness compared to standard state-constrained MPC and reactive safety filtering, while maintaining competitive task performance. The full implementation and experiments are available on the project website.

Motivation: 多机器人系统的运动规划通常计算量巨大，现有方法速度受限，难以满足实时性需求，需要高效的并行算法提升规划速度。

On pure multi-robot motion validation tests, this achieves over 1100X speedup in validation time. Additionally, we modify a representative set of MRMP algorithms to use these new primitives. ### [353] [Betting for Sim-to-Real Performance Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24018)
*Zaid Mahboob,Yujia Chen,Bowen Weng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出一种基于“下注”机制的新方法，用于在物理实验受限条件下高效、准确地评估机器人现实世界性能，并理论上优于传统蒙特卡罗估计方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实机器人实验昂贵且受限，获取精确性能评估非常困难，而高质量评估对于算法基准测试、系统设计、控制器验证和合规决策都至关重要。现有的仿真到现实（sim-to-real）方法虽然常被使用，但在估计方差、修正偏差方面存在局限性，因而亟需新的解决思路。

Method: 作者借鉴“下注”机制，推导出在一定理论条件下，如何通过构建投注策略来获得比蒙特卡罗法更高效、更准确的表现评估，并给出了近似实现方式和诊断决策规则。方法在合成数据和多保真度仿真平台上进行了实验验证。

Result: 所提的下注方法在理论上和实证上均优于常规的基准方法，如蒙特卡罗估计——在有效利用仿真信息补充稀缺的真实实验数据方面表现突出，并成功应用到机械臂抓取精度等实际任务。

Conclusion: 下注机制为sim-to-real机器人性能评估提供了新颖且高效的工具，能有效提升评估准确性并减少现实实验需求，对机器人研究和应用具有重要价值。

Abstract: This paper studies the problem of robot performance evaluation, focusing on how to obtain accurate and efficient estimates of real-world behavior under severe constraints on physical experimentation. Such estimates are essential for benchmarking algorithms, comparing design alternatives, validating controllers, and supporting certification or regulatory decision-making, yet real-world testing with physical robots is often expensive, time-consuming, and safety-limited. To mitigate the scarcity of real-world trials, sim-to-real methodologies are commonly employed, using low-cost simulators to inform, supplement, or prioritize physical experiments. Departing from (and complementary to) existing approaches in variance reduction (e.g., importance-sampling variants) or bias-correction (e.g., through prediction-powered inference or learned control variates), we examine this performance-evaluation problem through the lens of betting. We establish theoretical conditions under which a betting mechanism can yield accurate and efficient estimates (provably outperforming the Monte Carlo estimator) and we characterize how such bets should be constructed. We further develop theoretically grounded yet practically implementable approximations of the ideal bet, and we provide concrete decision rules that diagnose when these approximate betting strategies are working as intended. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methods using both synthetic examples and cross-fidelity computational simulators. Notably, we also showcase an illustrative case in which a group of synthetic distributions are used to infer the real-world pick-and-place accuracy of a robotic manipulator, a seemingly unconventional sim-to-real transfer that becomes natural and feasible under the proposed betting perspective. Programs for reproducing empirical results are available at https://github.com/ISUSAIL/Bet4Sim2Real.

</details>


### [354] [Event-based SLAM Benchmark for High-Speed Maneuvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24033)
*Sheng Zhong,Junkai Niu,Guillermo Gallego,Kaizhen Sun,Yang Yi,Zhiqiang Miao,Dewen Hu,Yaonan Wang,Davide Scaramuzza,Yi Zhou*

TL;DR: 本文对现有事件相机的视觉/视觉惯性里程计（VO/VIO）方法在极端机动场景下的表现进行了全面分析，并提出了用于评测的基准框架EvSLAM。该框架涵盖多平台、多照明和多运动模式，佐以新颖的评测指标，以寻找事件相机的最优解决方案，并揭示目前的挑战。

Method: 作者详尽分析了最先进的事件相机VO/VIO方法及现有公开数据集存在的短板。随后，提出了EvSLAM基准框架，包含多样化采集平台、极端光照和复杂运动类型，并引入新评估指标，对各方法在高动态机动条件下进行公平、系统的评价。

Result: EvSLAM基准框架可有效评测并对比各种事件相机方法，帮助发现其优势、最优架构及局限性；同时揭示现有数据集未覆盖的挑战与事件相机尚未充分解决的问题。

Abstract: Event-based cameras are bio-inspired sensors with pixels that independently and asynchronously respond to brightness changes at microsecond resolution, offering the potential to handle visual tasks in high-speed maneuvering scenarios. Existing event-based approaches, although successful in mitigating motion blur caused by high-speed maneuvers, suffer from many limitations. Some of them highlight a success of pose tracking for a fronto-parallel fast shaking camera closed to the structure, while others assume pure (optionally aggressive) three-degree-of-freedom rotations. The former requires persistent local map visibility within the field of view (FOV), whereas the latter fails to generalize to six-degree-of-freedom (6-DoF) motions where both linear and angular velocities may be large. Consequently, current successes do not fully demonstrate that event-based state estimation under arbitrary aggressive maneuvers is a fully solved problem. To quantitatively assess the extent to which the potential of event cameras has been unlocked, we conduct a thorough analysis of state-of-the-art (SOTA) event-based visual odometry (VO)/visual-inertial odometry (VIO) methods and report shortcomings in current public datasets. Furthermore, we introduce a benchmarking framework for event-based state estimation, called EvSLAM, characterized by sufficient variation in data collection platforms, diverse extreme lighting scenarios, and a wide scope of challenging motion patterns under a clear and rigorous definition of high-speed maneuvers for mobile robots, along with a novel evaluation metric designed to fairly assess the operational limits of event-based solutions. This framework benchmarks state-of-the-art methods, yielding insights into optimal architectures and persistent challenges.

Method: 扩展了标准MPCC方法，使其支持根据驾驶场景对车辆锚点（如牵引车前后轴与半挂车轴）分配不同权重，并在优化过程中对各关键车轴显式引入道路边界约束，确保所有受控车轮始终在可行驶区域内。

Abstract: This paper presents a trajectory planning method for articulated commercial vehicles, specifically tractor-semitrailers, based on Model Predictive Contouring Control (MPCC). Although MPCC has proven effective for passenger cars, it is generally ill-suited for tractor-semitrailers. These vehicles are significantly larger, the semitrailer follows a different path than the tractor, and reversing maneuvers are unstable and prone to jackknifing. Furthermore, practical driving scenarios often require scenario-dependent prioritization of different vehicle `anchor points', e.g., prioritizing the semitrailer position during docking or the tractor position when parking to charge. Therefore, we extend MPCC to enable scenario-dependent weighting of these anchor points and incorporate explicit road-boundary constraints for the front and rear tractor axles and the semitrailer axle, thereby ensuring that all considered wheels remain within the drivable area. The simulation results demonstrate the successful navigation of a representative logistic scenario in both forward and reverse direction.
